 jab raashtrapati ke aar narayanan ne 12 march 1998 ko jab atal bihari vaajapeyi ko sarkaar banane ke liye aamantrit kiya tha, tab ek saaf or sanvaidhanik misaal kaayam kar di thi
 Surjewala also cited an example of a part of KR Narayanan's letter which states that 'when no party or pre-poll alliance parties have a clear majority, the head of state is the first occasion party in India or anywhere and groups of parties Give it to the one who has won the most seats
 jise ek nishchit samay ke bheetar sadan ke patal par bahumat sabit karne kaa mauka diya jaae
 ' kya bijepi party tod kar sarkaar banaaegi, bahumat kahaan se laaegi

 bies yediurppake saath anant kumaar, saansad shobhaa karandalaaje, rajeev chandsekhar rajbhavan milane gaye

 bijepi pravaktaa ne bataaya ki rajyapal ne hamaara daawa to le liya magar koi taarikh nahin di

 yediurppa ne kaha ki sarkaar sau fisadi bijepi kii hi banegi
